CREATE DATABASE IF NOT EXISTS walmart;
USE walmart;

MariaDB [walmart_db]> CREATE TABLE train (
    ->     Store INT,
    ->     Dept INT,
    ->     Date DATE,
    ->     Weekly_Sales DECIMAL(10,2),
    ->     IsHoliday BOOLEAN
    -> );

MariaDB [walmart_db]> LOAD DATA INFILE 'D:/DA/data-analyst-portfolio/New folder/train.csv'
    -> INTO TABLE train
    -> FIELDS TERMINATED BY ','
    -> LINES TERMINATED BY '\n'
    -> IGNORE 1 ROWS
    -> (Store, Dept, Date, Weekly_Sales, IsHoliday);

Join train with stores → analyze by store type & size

Join train with features → analyze economic/weather factors TOP 10 Sales

MariaDB [walmart_db]> SELECT t.Store, t.Dept, f.Temperature, f.Fuel_Price, f.CPI, f.Unemployment,
    ->        SUM(t.Weekly_Sales) AS Total_Sales
    -> FROM train t
    -> JOIN features f
    ->   ON t.Store = f.Store AND t.Date = f.Date
    -> GROUP BY t.Store, t.Dept
    -> ORDER BY Total_Sales DESC
    -> LIMIT 10;

+-------+------+-------------+------------+------------+--------------+-------------+
| Store | Dept | Temperature | Fuel_Price | CPI        | Unemployment | Total_Sales |
+-------+------+-------------+------------+------------+--------------+-------------+
|    14 |   92 |       27.31 |      2.784 | 181.871189 | 8.992        | 26101497.71 |
|     2 |   92 |       40.19 |      2.572 | 210.752605 | 8.324        | 23572153.03 |

SELECT SUM(Weekly_Sales) AS Total_Sales
    -> FROM train
    -> INTO OUTFILE 'D:/DA/data-analyst-portfolio/New folder/total_sales.csv'
    -> FIELDS TERMINATED BY ','
    -> ENCLOSED BY '"'
    -> LINES TERMINATED BY '\n';

SELECT Store, SUM(Weekly_Sales) AS Store_Sales
    -> FROM train
    -> GROUP BY Store
    -> ORDER BY Store_Sales DESC
    -> INTO OUTFILE 'D:/DA/data-analyst-portfolio/New folder/store_sales.csv'
    -> FIELDS TERMINATED BY ','
    -> ENCLOSED BY '"'
    -> LINES TERMINATED BY '\n';

SELECT IsHoliday, SUM(Weekly_Sales) AS Total_Sales
    -> FROM train
    -> GROUP BY IsHoliday
    -> INTO OUTFILE 'D:/DA/data-analyst-portfolio/New folder/holiday_sales.csv'
    -> FIELDS TERMINATED BY ','
    -> ENCLOSED BY '"'
    -> LINES TERMINATED BY '\n';

SELECT Dept, DATE_FORMAT(Date, '%Y-%m') AS Month, AVG(Weekly_Sales) AS Avg_Sales
    -> FROM train
    -> GROUP BY Dept, Month
    -> ORDER BY Dept, Month
    -> INTO OUTFILE 'D:/DA/data-analyst-portfolio/New folder/dept_monthly_avg_sales.csv'
    -> FIELDS TERMINATED BY ','
    -> ENCLOSED BY '"'
    -> LINES TERMINATED BY '\n';

 SELECT Store, Dept, SUM(Weekly_Sales) AS Dept_Sales,
    ->        RANK() OVER (PARTITION BY Store ORDER BY SUM(Weekly_Sales) DESC) AS Dept_Rank
    -> FROM train
    -> GROUP BY Store, Dept
    -> INTO OUTFILE 'D:/DA/data-analyst-portfolio/New folder/dept_rank_per_store.csv'
    -> FIELDS TERMINATED BY ','
    -> ENCLOSED BY '"'
    -> LINES TERMINATED BY '\n';
